***ruien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruien.html>ruien</a> (67688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>With regular syncope of intervocalic <i>-d-</i> from earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruien.html>ruiden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*ruden</i> (attested in derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a>). Probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*reudjaną</i>, whence archaic <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">reuten</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to uproot, clear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, an ablaut variant of Proto-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rudōną</i>, whence Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rooien.html>rooien</a></i>, German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:roden.html>roden</a></i>.
</p><p>Alternatively compare perhaps <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruit.html>ruit</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mange</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, regionally also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rui.html>rui</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruien.html>ruide</a></i>, from Proto-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrūþǭ</i>, as hair loss <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> one of the main symptoms of mange in animals. The latter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> probably related with Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">roof</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">scab</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, to which compare the variant <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ruiven</i> above (though the <i>-v-</i> can also be explained as the fortition of an epenthetic <i>-w-</i> in hiatus).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruien.html>ruien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to moult, to shed (of animals; lose a covering of fur, <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a> or skin etc.)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ruien.html>ruien</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li>(<a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vogels.html>vogels</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:regelmatig.html>regelmatige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijden.html>tijden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veren.html>veren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wisselen.html>wisselen</a>.
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vogels.html>vogels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ruien.html>geruid</a></b>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:meervoud.html>meervoud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rui.html>rui</a></li></ol>

***ruig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruig.html>ruig</a> (7837)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ruuch</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ru.html>ru</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rou</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rūh</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rū</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rūhaz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rūhwaz</i>. The original <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> ended in <i>-h-</i>, which disappeared between vowels, giving <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rū-</i> in the inflected forms in Old Dutch. This then <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> rise to an alternative uninflected form <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rū</i>, which developed into Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ru.html>ru</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rou</i>, modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruw.html>ruw</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rouw.html>rouw</a></i>. The original uninflected form <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> back-formed to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruig.html>ruig</a></i> based on other <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> with <i>-ch</i> in the uninflected form and <i>-g-</i> in inflected forms, similar to what happened to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruig.html>ruig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruiger.html>ruiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ruigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rough, rugged, bristly</li>
<li>raucous, boisterous</li></ol>

***ruiken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruiken.html>ruiken</a> (2307)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ruken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rūcan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*reukaną</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rieken.html>rieken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruiken.html>ruiken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>To smell (i.e. to perceive a smell)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alsof.html>alsof</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ruik.html>ruik</a></b> / <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bloemen.html>bloemen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alweer.html>alweer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bloeien.html>bloeien</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zon.html>zon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brandt.html>brandt</a></i>  |  It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> just as if I <b>smell</b> / That the flowers are blooming again / And the sun be again always burning. <small>(KvK <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zomer.html>Zomer</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a>)</small></dd></dl></li>
<li>To smell (i.e. to emit a smell)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:houthakker.html>houthakker</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rook.html>rook</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamille.html>kamille</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goedkope.html>goedkope</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:parfum.html>parfum</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The lumberjack <b><a href = vnd.unilang:smelt.html>smelt</a></b> like chamomile and cheap perfume.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ruilen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruilen.html>ruilen</a> (3183)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ruylen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">roylen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">roelen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">reulen</i>, of uncertain origin. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">roalje</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">ruilje</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">reilen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">rülen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruilen.html>ruilen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruil.html>ruil</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruilen.html>ruilen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to swap, exchange</li>
<li>to trade</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***ruim.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruim.html>ruim</a> (1772)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ruum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rūm</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rūmaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruim.html>ruim</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruimer.html>ruimer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ruimst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>spacious, roomy
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eng.html>eng</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nauw.html>nauw</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krap.html>krap</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>large, wide</li>
<li>ample, generous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:portie.html>portie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ruim.html>ruim</a></b> bemeten.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That portion <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>amply</b> measured.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruim.html>ruim</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>more than, <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, easily
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weegt.html>weegt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ruim.html>ruim</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> ton.</i>
<dl><dd>It weighs <b><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></b> a ton.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ruum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rūm</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rūmą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruim.html>ruim</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruimen.html>ruimen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruim.html>ruimpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with definite article</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The wide, open space</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cargo hold</li></ol>

***ruimen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruimen.html>ruimen</a> (3903)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rumen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rūmen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rūmijaną</i>. Derived from the adjective <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rūmaz</i> and/or the noun <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rūmą</i>, from which Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruim.html>ruim</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruimen.html>ruimen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make more spacious</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to empty, to evacuate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put away, to tidy up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of farm animals</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cull, to exterminate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">typically for public health reasons</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruimen.html>ruimen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruim.html>ruim</a></i></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ruimen.html>ruimen</a></b>
</p>

***ruimte.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruimte.html>ruimte</a> (977)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rumede</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">space</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruim.html>ruim</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruimte.html>ruimte</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruimtes.html>ruimtes</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">ruimten</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>space, room for a physical object to occupy</li>
<li>room in a building
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vertrek.html>vertrek</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">normally with the definite article</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> space, outer space</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***ruit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruit.html>ruit</a> (9838)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rute</i>, of uncertain origin. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Raute</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruit.html>ruit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruiten.html>ruiten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruitje.html>ruitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geometry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The shape <span class="Latn" lang="en">rhombus</span>, an <span class="Latn" lang="en">equilateral</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">parallelogram</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">lozenge</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">diamond</span>; mostly used in the plural: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ruiten.html>ruiten</a></i>, for that <span class="Latn" lang="en">card suit</span></li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">glass</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:panel.html>panel</a></span> (as) in a <span class="Latn" lang="en">window</span>; hence, the whole window</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rute</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rūta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ῥυτή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rhutḗ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruit.html>ruit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruiten.html>ruiten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruitje.html>ruitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A plant of the genus <i>Ruta</i>; rue.</li>
<li>One of a number of similar plants, notably the related <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Thalictrum_flava" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Thalictrum flava"><i>Thalictrum flava</i></a></span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any <span class="Latn" lang="en">weed</span>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruit.html>ruit</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">second- and third-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruien.html>ruien</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention"> plural imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruien.html>ruien</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ruit.html>ruit</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
